Discovery.

In validation testing, ARBITER independently identified a billion-dollar drug pathway — without training data, in under one second.

Our deterministic validation engine doesn't just check existing recommendations. By mapping the full semantic coherence space between molecular targets and therapeutic mechanisms, ARBITER surfaces novel pathways that traditional screening misses.

No training data. No historical examples. Pure semantic coherence.
